How Much Is A Billion?

Comprehending The Worth of a Billion Dollars

By: Paul McBurney Jr

Tweet

$999000000

The human brain is dumb. If we truly want to comprehend how big $1B is, our visualization needs to be 1 Dimensional. And the only way to do that, is to utilize just one thing. The emoji...

But Wait!

Before we lead up to a billion dollars, lets visualize expensive things that a billionaire could buy. For example, this multi-million dollar mansion costs...

$30,000,000

To put 30 million into perspective (which is a lot less than 1 Billion) lets pretend that one:

💵 = $10,000

💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 💵 Wow! Thats a lot of $10,000 Bills. Did I mention that it takes the Average American 2 Years to save $10,000 dollars? (Just one bill on the screen)

Now that we've got a mansion out of the way. A billionaire might want a lavish mode of transportation! How about a Boeing 737 that costs nearly...

$100,000,000

To put $100,000,000 into perspective, lets pretend that one 💵 emoji represents $10,000 dollars. If that's the case, it would take this many emojis to purchase that plane!
